<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:soil.html>soil</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:earth.html>earth</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ground.html>ground</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:apple.html>apple</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> <i>earthapple</i>; <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pomme <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terre.html>terre</a></i>, Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Gromper</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:ground.html>ground</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pear.html>pear</a>"), <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> regionally <a href = vnd.unilang:both.html>both</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Erdapfel</i> ("<a href = vnd.unilang:earth.html>earth</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:apple.html>apple</a>") <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grundbirne</i> ("<a href = vnd.unilang:ground.html>ground</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pear.html>pear</a>")

***aarde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a> (794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āerde</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ertha</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*erþō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardes.html>aardes</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aardetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***aardig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardig.html>aardig</a> (492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***abacus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abacus.html>abacus</a> (77566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:abacus.html>abacus</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄβαξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ábax</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:abominabel.html>abominabel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">abhominabel</i>, borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:abominable.html>abominable</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">abominabilis</i>.

</p>
